####THE RISE OF THE GREAT MING#####
####Not all of House Zhu is rendered outside the immediate family of the Emperors and any previous consort preceding the birth of the next emperor

8001000 = { #Hongwu Emperor (lived 1320-1398) (reigned 1368)
	dynasty = 8001000 #Zhu

	religion = ruist
	culture = mandarin

	trait = sympathy_islam
	#born to a peasant family rose to power during the Turban Rebellion and the Displacement of the Yuan Emperors
	1328.10.21 = {birth = yes}
	1368.1.23 = {
		name = "Hongwu"
		add_spouse = 8001002 #Empress Xiaocigao (Ma)
	}
	1398.6.24 = {death = { death_reason = death_offmap }}
}

#########The Great Qing Empire######################

#####NOTES: The Manchu is a later name given to what was then called Jurchen but for brevity they are all Manchu as was the ancient Jin Dynasty of the 13th century
#####Qing Nobility was organized to banners and ranks much like the Yuan Emperors and other Mongol Cliques
#####Not all the Kids of Emperors are included for the sake of my sanity and tbh not all matter (Sorry Iron Princes and First Rank Fans)
#####As such the game will only render the primary consorts of note such as those relevant to the Next Emperors succession
#####i.e. (Empress Dowagers, Empresses and primary consorts that the Emperor Liked)
